  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_2677a6ee-91e2-4f49-97b5-13c0d8ff8242'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

Jaded & enigmatic Andrew Hamilton’s rather UN-reasonable to reaction to discovering his new intern deceived him!</b><br/><br/><u>There are 3 parts to the Reasonable Doubt serial, which should be read in order:</u><br/><b>Part 1: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/898609990' rel='nofollow noopener'>Reasonable Doubt</a><br/>Part 2: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/898610453' rel='nofollow noopener'>Reasonable Doubt II</a><br/>Part 3: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/904001041' rel='nofollow noopener'>Reasonable Doubt III</a><br/>Part 3.1: <a href='http://www.whitneygracia.com/2014/09/reasonable-doubt-3-extended-epilogue.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Extended epilogue</a></b><br/><br/><b>Reasonable Doubt</b> (part 1) is man-whore extraordinaire, attorney and law firm partner, <b>Andrew Hamilton</b>’s story. It follows him <b>six years after gut-wrenching be</b></span>
  <span id="freeText2184093549543832343" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/WiliamsReasonabledoubtTitebySueBee_zps4fc749ed.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397113562ra/9232990.gif" alt=" photo RDstoryxBbysb_zps1d3540d7.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>★★★★★! Unreasonable Doubt (part 1). Jaded &amp; enigmatic Andrew Hamilton’s rather UN-reasonable to reaction to discovering his new intern deceived him!</b><br><br><u>There are 3 parts to the Reasonable Doubt serial, which should be read in order:</u><br><b>Part 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/898609990" rel="nofollow noopener">Reasonable Doubt</a><br>Part 2: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/898610453" rel="nofollow noopener">Reasonable Doubt II</a><br>Part 3: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/904001041" rel="nofollow noopener">Reasonable Doubt III</a><br>Part 3.1: <a href="http://www.whitneygracia.com/2014/09/reasonable-doubt-3-extended-epilogue.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Extended epilogue</a></b><br><br><b>Reasonable Doubt</b> (part 1) is man-whore extraordinaire, attorney and law firm partner, <b>Andrew Hamilton</b>’s story. It follows him <b>six years after gut-wrenching betrayal</b> that forced him away from his previous life, details to be unfolding with story. He has settled into a comfortable life of practicing law and his free time spent on the various internet dating sites for <b>his next one-night-stand</b>.<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“This is always the most annoying part, the part when the woman who previously agreed to “One dinner. One night. No repeats.” wants to establish some type of imaginary connection.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>For the past six months he has been <b>offering legal advice</b> to Alyssa, a young new lawyer in his city and, though they never met, they have formed a <b>friendship of sorts</b>. Though she doesn’t want to meet him and insists on being unattractive part of him still <b>wants to hit it</b>, just once… <br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I’ve never fucked one of my friends before.” <br>“That’s because I’m your only one.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>Then upon <b>sitting in at the final interviews</b>, for the coveted intern position at his firm, he meets a young attractive pre-law student, Aubrey Everhart. And yet again <b>he discovers he has been deceived</b>….<br><br><b>Reasonable Doubt</b> will follow Andrew in his somewhat <b>UN-reasonable reaction</b> to the <b>unraveling of</b> he is perfectly <b>organized and carnal</b> existence providing for <b>off-the-charts sex</b> and a chance of a glimpse of his <b>infamous cock</b>.<br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIFS%20for%20my%20reads/RDHxBbysb_zpsce6459b6.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397113562ra/9232991.gif" alt=" photo RDHxBbysb_zpsce6459b6.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <b><br><a>ANDREW HAMILTON:</a><br>32 years/attorney/partner at Greenwood Bach &amp; Hamilton/$$$$/dark brown hair/blue eyes.</b>
</i><br><br>Seven words to describe <b>Andrew: Charismatic, jaded, flawed, commanding, enigmatic, vulnerable and larger-than-life</b>.<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I immediately clicked on my profile and opened the “What I’m Looking For” box, making sure that it still read the same: “Casual sex. Nothing more. Nothing Less.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIFS%20for%20my%20reads/RDhexBbysb_zpsd1c039cb.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397113562ra/9232992.gif" alt=" photo RDhexBbysb_zpsd1c039cb.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <b><br><a>AUBREY EVERHART:</a><br>22 years/pre-law student/blond hair/blue eyes/ballerina.</b>
</i><br><br>Seven words to describe <b> Aubrey Everhart: Smart, naïve, endearing, focused, lonely, impressionable and resilient</b>.<br><br><b>Reasonable Doubt</b> was the perfect read for me. Both Andrew and Aubrey might have been a little slow at catching on to the truth, but that’s how it needed to be. Story moved along at a <b>fast pace</b> only to come to a <b>shocking mother-of-all cliffys</b> ending. Thankfully part 2: <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/898610453" rel="nofollow noopener">Reasonable Doubt II</a>
</b> should be out shortly! [wipes sweat!]<br><br><b>Excellent</b> story-telling! <b>Entertaining</b> dialogue! <b>Captivating</b> plot! <b>Steamy</b> sex scenes! <b>Swoon-worthy</b> hero, Andrew Hamilton! <b>Compelling</b> heroine! <b>5 sexxxy</b> stars!<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Is there super-glue on my floor? Is that why you’re still standing there?”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>***<br>Hero rating: 5 stars <br>Heroine rating: 5 stars<br>Sex scenes rating: 5 stars<br>Sex scenes frequency: 4.5 stars<br>Storyline concept rating: 4.5 stars<br>Storytelling skills rating: 5 stars<br>Story ending rating: N/A<br>Book editing rating (5 = no edits spotted): 5 stars<br>************************************************<br><b>Overall rating: 5 stars<br><br>Would I recommend this series: Yes.<br>Would I re-read this series: Yes.<br>Would I read future books by this author: Yes.</b><br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIFS%20for%20my%20reads/sexyembraceTuNvxBbysb_zpse5641e8d.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

He is quickly making his way through the ladies of the internet spending a week ensuring they who they say they are. But one women he meets online, not on a dating site, seems to pull his attention. She's the only woman not after his cock, not after a relationship... just a little professional assistance. </a><br><br>So let me try to get my tongue back in my mouth here.... Holy fucking shit was this a hot little quick read! This was one of those <i>'don't think just click'</i> moments and it did not disappoint. Set in a three part serial format, the first installment is short; but it gets you to a fairly good point before the mother of all cliffhangers knocks you on your ass. But have no fear, it appears that these will be released with about a two week timeline. <br><br>Now on to the shit that makes your panties wet. Andrew is an asshole. He's a man-whore jerk who likes to dirty talk. He just crossed the threshold into becoming a book boyfriend god with those four things checked off.<br><br> <i>
  <b> "The cherry he'd picked up was in his mouth, and he was pressing it on my lips - silently commanding me to open up and eat it. I stuck out my tongue to take it, but before sliding it to me, he whispered, "Don't chew... "I wanted her to ride me." He trailed his hand up my thigh and rubbed his thumb against my clit. "On my cock and my mouth. And I wanted to teach her how to taste me..."</b>
</i> <br><br>I don't know where Whitney Gracia Williams came from, but I am sure as shit glad she decided to write this erotica short series. There is a narrow window while writing in this format to really create something enjoyable. With such limited space for the story, the scenes and the characters it is more likely the case that something is left out, something that leaves the reader missing some key moment to bring the story together. Sure you can get sucked in with a blurb, you can keep the sex hot enough to cause the reader to squirm... but that is not rare. What WGW pulled off was giving you it all. This short read packed a punch and gave you everything that a novel three times its size could deliver.<br><br>I cannot wait to get my needy little hands on the next installment of this series. </span>

You know, the ones that may tell you that this may catch up with you one day. What was it one of your conquests recently told you? <b>Karma is on hell of a bitch.</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">I know. I fucker her two weeks ago...</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397683467ra/9311439.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And yet I find myself strangely turned on.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">I'd built the last six years of my life detaching myself from any chance of having feelings for someone else, <i>refusing</i> to build any friendships...</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>But didn't you make a friend...your only friend if I recall correctly. The one you met in the lawyer chat room but never met. What was her name? Alyssa? Was that it?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397683467ra/9311440.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yes I got all that, thank you. But you also find yourself wishing you were getting that pussy from Alyssa, don't you?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394592344ra/8875163.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Well then! No need to get bitchy! I can see you're a little touchy on this subject since she refuses to meet you or tell you her real name.<br><br>But then you DO meet someone. That new college intern...the one that happens to be EXACTLY your type. You just can't seem to stay away from her, can you? What's that relationship like? First you fight, and then all of a sudden there's some angry fuckery?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388080196ra/7734445.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yes, yes, I get it.<br><br>But she's also keeping something from you, isn't she?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397684173ra/9311665.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Right. You have that thing against someone being a fucking liar.<br><br>Oh but you're keeping something even bigger from here, aren't you? And what do you do? LEAVE US WITH A FUCKING CLIFFHANGER IS WHAT!!! GAH!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394665176ra/8885767.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now I'll just be slowly dying inside waiting for book 2 to see how redeemable your assholy-ness really is.<br><br>And I thank you<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397366603ra/9268038.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>For more reviews visit<br><a href="http://dirtygirlromance.blogspot.com/" target="blogspot" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436206i/881587.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br></b></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2604195942" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12253298589159612443">Andrew Hamilton was a high-profile lawyer working in a big lawyer firm in Nowhere, NC. <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1543194323i/26648385._SX540_.jpg' alt='Lawyer' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>He was obsessed with sex, loved one-night stands ending with one, and kept visiting all known online dating sites to find yet another woman to have sex with. The book blurb gives an excellent quote about him and I cannot help copying it here:<br/><i>My cock has an appetite.<br/><br/>A huge and very particular appetite: Blonde, curvy, and preferably not a fucking liar... </i><br/><br/>Aubrey Everhart was an undergraduate student majoring in l</span>
  <span id="freeText12253298589159612443" style="display:none">Andrew Hamilton was a high-profile lawyer working in a big lawyer firm in Nowhere, NC. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1543194323i/26648385._SX540_.jpg" alt="Lawyer" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>He was obsessed with sex, loved one-night stands ending with one, and kept visiting all known online dating sites to find yet another woman to have sex with. The book blurb gives an excellent quote about him and I cannot help copying it here:<br><i>My cock has an appetite.<br><br>A huge and very particular appetite: Blonde, curvy, and preferably not a fucking liar... </i><br><br>Aubrey Everhart was an undergraduate student majoring in law. She stumbled upon a web site for lawyers only, registered herself as a full lawyer and stumbled upon Andrew Hamilton. Posing as a newbie she managed to get him to consult her (regarding her undergrad assignments, but Andrew thought these were her real cases). She was also a hopeful ballerina.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1543194438i/26648393._SX540_.jpg" alt="Ballerina" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To make a long story short they started calling each other by phone and became virtual friends having no clue about each other identities. In the meantime Andrew's sexual frustration became really bad - obviously there were only limited amount of attractive women in Nowhere, NC willing to have sex with an outright asshole. <br><br>Andrew's frustration resulted in all of their talks with Aubrey being about one subject only: her genitalia and what he would do to it if they ever meet. Do I need to say that poor Aubrey was not too eager to do so - it should be obvious. In my opinion she was still weird as any normal woman can only listen for so long about her vagina before forcing her "admirer" into therapy. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1543194592i/26648407._SX540_.jpg" alt="Therapy" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In any other way Aubrey was quite a decent character and her only fault I could find was falling for a giant asshole with serious sexual problems. Here I came to the character of Andrew. He was referred to as an alpha, but in my humble opinion he was anything but. <b>Alphas do not get obsessed with female genitalia!!!</b> Below is an alpha, Andrew was not!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1543193662i/26648377._SX540_.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This guy definitely does not have Andrew's obsession. <br><br>Still one thought bothers me after I finished the book: considering Aubrey fell for Andrew does it mean I was trying to get the girls the wrong way when I was young? It looks like all I needed to do was talking about Andrew's favorite subject and any girl would jump at me right away. Can anybody confirm? <br><br>Andrew's character practically made me rate this books with two stars. However considering how many of my friends rated it much higher I increased the rating by one star; after all as I said I like Aubrey well enough. </span>

</b><br><br>I didn’t really care for this story. <br>The writing was iffy and confusing. <br>I was flat out bored page after page... <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492083805ra/22480312.gif" width="375" height="225" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Haha thanks Rihanna.<br><br><b>
  <i>”Once someone lies to me they’re dead to me forever.”</i>
</b><br><br>Come on Andrew Hamilton, you’ll get over it! <br><br>Andrew and Alyssa’s story so far was funny,steamy and I’m sure excited to see where Whitney Gracia Williams takes them next. It does indeed end with a cliffhanger and I’m hoping the next book magically appears published today!!<br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="5920905674618825173" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1928785806531973839">4.5 STARS!!<br/><br/>Okay...THAT WAS HOT! Don't even ask me why these jilted assholes interest me, I don't know! Probably nothing to be proud of anyway! <br/>But this was a spicy and hot little novella that proves great things come in small packages! The first in a series of three, RD was a fast paced and scorching read. Andrew is all about the one-nighters. His MO: Wine em' and dine them.<br/> Screw em' and leave em'.<br/><br/>It's working so far and for reasons we don't quite know yet, Andrew is escaping from a horrible pa</span>
  <span id="freeText1928785806531973839" style="display:none">4.5 STARS!!<br /><br />Okay...THAT WAS HOT! Don't even ask me why these jilted assholes interest me, I don't know! Probably nothing to be proud of anyway! <br />But this was a spicy and hot little novella that proves great things come in small packages! The first in a series of three, RD was a fast paced and scorching read. Andrew is all about the one-nighters. His MO: Wine em' and dine them.<br /> Screw em' and leave em'.<br /><br />It's working so far and for reasons we don't quite know yet, Andrew is escaping from a horrible past, possibly a horrible love gone bad. He doesn't tolerate relationships and will NEVER, EVER tolerate a liar. So quick, no work one night stints do him just fine. He's also been speaking to a woman, Alyssa, on a lawyers forum meant to connect people of that profession. She describes herself as unattractive but he wants her. Badly. Though he's never met her...yet.<br /><br />Until a new intern is hired at his law firm and everything is blown out the window! Talk about ruining the best laid plans!<br />This was so good! I loved every short page of it and can't wait for more!!!</span>

It hooks the reader right from the start. <br/><br/> <b>Andrew</b> has rules about the women he spends time with:<br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397571790i/9294533._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Until one particular lady, <b>Aubrey</b>, piques his interest and makes him reconsider his rules. The other half loved it."</b></i> Yes, Andrew, you summed up the book for me. <br/><br/><b>SERIES:</b><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20761374.Reasonable_Doubt_Volume_1__Reasonable_Doubt___1_' title='Reasonable Doubt Volume 1 (Reasonable Doubt, #1) by Whitney Gracia Williams' rel='nofollow noopener'>

I devour them and always want more. </b><br> <br>Andrew is partner at a law firm. He uses on-line dating to find no strings attached relationships. He doesn’t have any friends, except for one. Alyssa is a girl he met on-line. They kept an internet relationship for six months, but Andrew wants to meet her. Alyssa is hesitant.<br> <br><b>Review</b><br> <br>I didn’t know anything going into this book. I just knew there was a picture of a girl that was a ballerina and already that perked my interest.<br> <br><b>Andrew</b><br> <br>Sexy Andrew, what can I say, I love the name. Is it the same name as my husband? Maybe, but regardless, Whitney G. always writes dominate Heroes. Andrew is successful, powerful and knows what he wants and he wants Alyssa. I love the way he talks the way he presents himself, everything!<br> <br><b>Aubrey</b><br> <br>Adorable Aubrey. She’s a young something trying to double major in pre-law and ballet. She wants to be a ballerina, but her parents want her to be a lawyer. I really liked this. Her character is unique, in the sense she’s soft with a harsh exterior. She doesn’t want to mess up the relationship she has with Andrew so she never intends to meet him, but fate has other plans.<br> <br><b>Overall</b><br> <br>Book 1 is short, but it’s jam packed with stuff. There’s awesome banter between Aubrey and Andrew, sexy steamy scenes that is off the charts and just when I think the story can only go one way, it changes direction.<br> <br>I think what I liked so much about this part of the series is that it wasn’t typical. <span id="freeTextContainer18266462351809277956"><b>2.5 STARS<br/>Short and Steamy. <br/>That is how I would sum up this novella.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396515725i/9145997.png' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>"Casual sex. Nothing more. Nothing less." That's what our Andrew is interested in, and that's exactly what he's looking for at online dating sites. He is a lawyer who hates liars above everything. He is a man with only one friend Alyssa whom he has never seen face to face. But one interview at his place of work will change everything...<br/><blockquote>
  <i>"What do you look like?"<br/>"I look like a man who wants to f*ck you."</i>
</blockquote><br/>Brazen, confident, smart.</span>
  <span id="freeText18266462351809277956" style="display:none"><b>2.5 STARS<br>Short and Steamy. <br>That is how I would sum up this novella.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396515725i/9145997.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>"Casual sex. Nothing more. Nothing less." That's what our Andrew is interested in, and that's exactly what he's looking for at online dating sites. He is a lawyer who hates liars above everything. He is a man with only one friend Alyssa whom he has never seen face to face. But one interview at his place of work will change everything...<br><blockquote>
  <i>"What do you look like?"<br>"I look like a man who wants to f*ck you."</i>
</blockquote><br>Brazen, confident, smart. I really enjoyed reading about Andrew, about his dirty mouth and about the way he was "pinning" for Alyssa.<br><blockquote>
  <i>"I don't f*ck virgins. But considering the fact that you and I have never f*cked, you might as well be one."</i>
</blockquote><br>However, this novella didn't satisfy my cravings. Guess I'm not "serial" kind of reader. I wished there was more depth into the characters, more plot, more everything. I know there is more to come, and I plan on reading next instalment because of that killer cliffhanger, but I would prefer to read it all at once as a standalone full lenght novel. Plus there was this very visible plothole that bothered me a lot but since it is spoilery, I suggest not to read this spoiler if you haven't read book yet - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Alyssa/Aubrey was talking on phone with Andrew every day for 6 months. He was always honest with her, she knew his mentality, his talking patterns... So don't tell me that she wouldn't recognize Andrew's voice (or Andrew himself) once she started working for him... <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br><b>If short romance serial is your thing, go for it. I'm sure you'll find this novella very enjoayble.</b><br><br>MORE REVIEWS ON MY BLOG <a href="http://readingismybreathing.blogspot.cz/" rel="nofollow noopener">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer899021520" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16209279994350521202">***5 Thoreau Stars***<br/><br/>OMG..... Seriously I need BOOK 2 STAT!!!! How can you not love this novella... Hot sexy lawyer..Check.. Dirty talks..Check... Hot Sex...Check... Lies after Lies,...Check and a shocker for an ending..BIG FAT CHECK!!! Ummm...Ms. Whitney G., please don't make us wait too long for Book 2.. I need more Andrew and Aubrey!!!!!<br/><br/><a href='https://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/13606253934' title='reasonable doubt by ms.meesh, on Flickr' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396544460i/9149658.jpg' width='500' height='448' alt='reasonable doubt' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Andrew Hamilton is 32 years and a high profile lawyer. He is smart, sexy, and one hell of a dirty talker. He only has three simple rules to abide by when </span>
  <span id="freeText16209279994350521202" style="display:none">***5 Thoreau Stars***<br><br>OMG..... Seriously I need BOOK 2 STAT!!!! How can you not love this novella... Hot sexy lawyer..Check.. Dirty talks..Check... Hot Sex...Check... Lies after Lies,...Check and a shocker for an ending..BIG FAT CHECK!!! Ummm...Ms. Whitney G., please don't make us wait too long for Book 2.. I need more Andrew and Aubrey!!!!!<br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/13606253934" title="reasonable doubt by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396544460i/9149658.jpg" width="500" height="448" alt="reasonable doubt" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Andrew Hamilton is 32 years and a high profile lawyer. He is smart, sexy, and one hell of a dirty talker. He only has three simple rules to abide by when it comes to women: <b><br>One Dinner, One Night. No Repeats. </b> Also, another big NO NO NO for Andrew is that he hates <b> LIARS</b>. For him, once you lie...its sayonara! Simple as that!<br><br>Andrew doesn't have many friends and the only one friend he considers is his <i> Alyssa</i>, who happens to be a 27 year old lawyer who has red hair and green eyes that he met on LawChat. For the past six months, they have been conversing over emails, text messages and on the phone. They have developed this flirtatious friendship. Alyssa would ask Andrew for legal advice on cases that she is working on. Through this ongoing friendship, Andrew makes it clear that he wants to meet her but Alyssa always avoids it. <br><br>When Andrew and his partners are interviewing for new interns for the firm, a beautiful 22 year old comes walking into the board room. Aubrey is a junior at Duke University and interviewing for an internship. As they are conducting the interview, Andrew notices that answers Aubrey were giving were the same questions "Alyssa" was asking him. Putting two and two together, Andrew discovers his Alyssa is Aubrey. Lying is the number one thing Andrew despises. When Andrew finally clues Aubrey that he is aware of her lies, let the office madness and shenanigans begin. <br><br>Reasonable Doubt is just WOW!! This quick steamy novella has me imploring for more...I need to know what happens next. This is my first read of Ms. Whitney Gracia Williams and I will definitely be checking out of her other books. The writing was exceptional. Dialogues were funny, witty, sexy and entertaining. And I adore the characters. Andrew was just oozing with sexiness and Aubrey/Alyssa was lovable. Holy hell...this short novella by Ms. Whitney has me begging for more. That ending....ugh!! I need you to hurry up, finish writing book 2 and hit publish! <br><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6518370.Whitney_Gracia_Williams" title="Whitney Gracia Williams" rel="nofollow noopener">Whitney Gracia Williams</a></span>

</a><br><br><br>Andrew is a corporate partner of a lawyers company, so how does he find his women with his work requiring long hours? He does online dating with a secret name. <br><br><br><b>ONE NIGHT, that's it, his only RULE.</b><br><br><br>Aubrey loves to <b>DANCE</b>, she has been dancing since she was 6, it's her dream but she also needs money to do her dream, to survive she is required to double major half dance, half Law.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/75921005-C022-4865-A669-9BCA8C65E002_zpsmhkrc4ds.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><br>Aubrey has a big workload not much time to socialise and not much time to meet people, so she goes to an online lawyers dating blog where she meets people of same likeness as her. Aubrey has no friends, her family aren't interested in Aubrey being happy but more importantly keeping their family as lawyers going, but she wants to achieve her goals on her own without having to work in her parents company  so the only way to gain the finances she needs of her parents in order to continue her dream is to find her own way and get a position in a firm as a pre-law student. <b>She needs BALANCE</b><br><br><br>And therefore where Aubrey and Andrew meet for six months online and likewise where Andrew has yet again been deceived in real person.<br><br><br><b>My thoughts</b><br><br>LOVE, LOVE, LOVED IT.   function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('LsSIRHh/ksPl9ddzzQk7CKcOmitg4kl/PLy4WiX1fHTetA0MNhXPQHv+nc3B1YfvighInhvKQh1lAS86TTxbxg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Y09jMGAXR4JjLXn7isfB9H92q1Kw/p451QY6qytuvueTP+Z4Ln0aAf0mM0WGG30TUnB558vWlVuMu63LQ6eZVQ==')})
  }
